        (function(){

            return;

          window.listViewFirstAvailabilityResponse = new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {

            var requestUrl = "/s-accommodations/api/accommodations/availability?from=SB2&limit=21&destination_id=CIT_6890&checkin=2021-03-31&checkout=2021-04-01&distribution=2&quick=true&token=oZ702fVJVR&page=1&real_traffic=true";

            xhr.setRequestHeader("search-id", "f0e397ff-b822-4fbb-8d42-2babe46c4a38");xhr.setRequestHeader("flow", "shopping");xhr.setRequestHeader("step-flow", "results");xhr.setRequestHeader("product", "hotels");xhr.setRequestHeader("x-client", "s-accommodations");xhr.setRequestHeader("page-view-id", "shopping-accommodations-it-a3b97625-e0ca-4f71-9c2f-5cd5eabdb71d");xhr.setRequestHeader("x-hash", "dGO9NbDPpls1mDLvUbdL6Z2XM1vgjVauQ%2BYt6IZAi%2BZWI2tggvbxCaKoNTSnDPMnpwcb2ifoMgkLf1IicggsYg%3D%3D");xhr.setRequestHeader("x-user-id", "67487d15-a004-4e97-887d-15a0044e970c");xhr.setRequestHeader("upa-tracking", "pageview");

            xhr.onload = function () {
              if (!!window.performance && !!window.performance.mark) {
                performance.mark('end_availability_request');
              }

              var json = function(responseText) {
                try {
                  return JSON.parse(responseText);
                } catch (e) {
                  return null;
                }
              }

              var parseHeaders = function(headers) {
                var arr = headers.trim().split(/[\r\n]+/);

                // Create a map of header names to values
                var headerMap = {};
                arr.forEach(function (line) {
                  var parts = line.split(': ');
                  var header = parts.shift();
                  var value = parts.join(': ');
                  headerMap[header] = value;
                });

                return headerMap;
              }

              var data = json(xhr.responseText);

              var response = {
                'data': data,
                'requestParams': {"page":1,"reason":"pageview"},
                'acceptQuick': true,
                'status': xhr.status,
                'statusText': xhr.statusText,
                'headers': parseHeaders(xhr.getAllResponseHeaders()),
                'url': requestUrl,
              };

              if (xhr.status === 200 && data !== null) {
                resolve(response);
              } else {
                reject(response);
              }
            };

            xhr.onerror = function() {
              if (!!window.performance && !!window.performance.mark) {
                performance.mark('end_availability_request');
              }

              var response = {
                'data': null,
                'requestParams': {"page":1,"reason":"pageview"},
                'acceptQuick': true,
                'status': xhr.status,
                'statusText': xhr.statusText,
                'url': requestUrl,
              };
              reject(response);
            };

            if (!!window.performance && !!window.performance.mark) {
              performance.mark('start_availability_request');
            }

            xhr.send();
          });
        })();
